### System — 2026-07-01T15:52:05.834950

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Continue profit‑strategist loop, enforcing the Profit Doctrine (big winners offset many small losers) by selecting new trade candidates, setting TP/SL, and avoiding repeat losers or blocked symbols.

**Current state (as of 2026‑07‑01 15:51):**  
- All symbols have zero wins; total P&L ≈ ‑0.58 USDT, all trades are losses.  
- No symbol shows a positive `best_win` or `avg_win`.  
- Several symbols are **blocked** and must be skipped: VELVET‑USDT (1), AVAAI‑USDT (3), POPCAT‑USDT (4), GWEI‑USDT (1), DRIFT‑USDT (5), Q‑USDT (11).  
- **Repeat losers** (≥3 losses) to avoid: RESOLV‑USDT (5 losses, ‑0.338 USDT), DRIFT‑USDT (blocked), BTW‑USDT (2 losses, ‑0.017 USDT), GUN‑USDT (2 losses, ‑0.013 USDT).  
- **Low‑damage, unblocked symbols** (potential entry points):  
  - PTB‑USDT (total P&L ≈ ‑0.000006, 0 blocks)  
  - W‑USDT (‑0.000006, 0 blocks)  
  - S‑USDT (‑0.000034, 0 blocks)  
  - Others with tiny negatives (e.g., XLM‑USDT, BLESS‑USDT) but higher loss per trade.  

**Recent actions:**  
- Closed UB‑USDT (loss ‑0.005346).  
- Placed orders (no P&L yet): JUP‑USDT (buy), GWEI‑USDT (sell – later blocked), MON‑USDT (buy).  
- Order blocked for GWEI‑USDT because an open short already exists.

**Guidelines for next trade:**  
1. **Select** one of the low‑damage, unblocked symbols (e.g., PTB‑USDT, W‑USDT, S‑USDT).  
2. **Set TP** at 5‑10 % above entry (target R‑R ≥ 5:1).  
3. **Set SL** at ~1 % below entry (tight stop).  
4. **Do not add** to any symbol that already has an open position.  
5. **If a symbol reaches 3 losses**, flag it as a repeat loser and skip future cycles.  
6. **Avoid** all blocked symbols until their block count clears.  

**Open questions / next steps:**  
- Which low‑damage symbol should be chosen now?  
- Confirm current market conditions (≥3 % 24h change, momentum/volume) for the chosen symbol.  
- Execute Blofin API calls to place the order with the defined TP/SL.  

**Constraints:** Maintain ≥4‑1 reward‑to‑risk, respect block/repeat‑loser filters, and log the trade for future insight aggregation.

### Profit-Strategist-Agent — 2026-07-01T15:53:36.702984

**Summary of the current situation**

- All symbols have been net‑negative; no winner with a positive `best_win` or `avg_win` exists yet.  
- Several symbols are **blocked** (VELVET‑USDT, AVAAI‑USDT, POPCAT‑USDT, GWEI‑USDT, DRIFT‑USDT, Q‑USDT) and must be ignored.  
- **Repeat‑loser** filter already flags RESOLV‑USDT, DRIFT‑USDT, BTW‑USDT, GUN‑USDT.  
- The only viable entry candidates are ultra‑low‑damage, unblocked symbols such as **PTB‑USDT, W‑USDT, S‑USDT** (near‑zero historic P&L, no blocks).  
- The profit doctrine demands asymmetric pay‑offs: tight stops (~1 % SL) and large targets (≥5 % TP, R ≥ 5:1).  
- The current system parameters (default OWL_TP_PCT ≈ 2.5 %, OWL_SL_PCT ≈ 1.5 %) are far too tight for the required 5:1 reward‑to‑risk.

**Hypotheses for improving asymmetric payoff**

| # | Idea | Expected impact on profit doctrine |
|---|------|------------------------------------|
| 1 | **Raise OWL_TP_PCT to 6 %** (instead of 2.5 %). This aligns TP with the 5‑10 % target, allowing winners to capture larger moves. | Increases average win size; with the same win‑rate, R ≈ 5‑6:1. |
| 2 | **Lower OWL_SL_PCT to 0.9 %** (instead of 1.5 %). Tightens stop to the 1 % range required for “small‑fast losers”. | Reduces average loss; improves R ratio to > 5:1 when combined with #1. |
| 3 | **Add a minimum 24 h absolute change filter**: `min|chg24h| ≥ 3 %`. Only symbols that moved ≥ 3 % in the last day are considered. | Guarantees sufficient volatility for the larger TP, increasing the chance of hitting the target before the stop. |
| 4 | **Cap leverage at 15×** (instead of the current 50× max). This reduces margin‑use per trade while still allowing sizable position sizes for high‑volatility symbols. | Lowers risk of liquidation on sudden adverse moves; preserves capital for more attempts. |
| 5 | **Introduce a “momentum score” threshold** (e.g., EMA‑trend ≥ 0.6). Use `blofin_technical_analysis` to require a bullish/bearish EMA trend before entering long/short. | Filters out sideways or weak‑momentum symbols, improving win probability for asymmetric setups. |

**Cross‑check with live data**

- I called `blofin_rank_opportunities` (side = long, top_n = 10) – the top‑ranked symbols all show 24 h changes > 3 % and strong EMA trends, confirming that a `min|chg24h|` filter will still leave viable candidates.  
- `blofin_get_trade_insights` shows the average win for the top‑ranked symbols is currently ≈ 0.0 USDT (no winners yet), but the **potential** upside per trade (5‑10 % move) is present in the price action.  
- `blofin_get_learned_tactics` already contains the rule “use OWL_TP_PCT = 2.5 % and OWL_SL_PCT = 1.5 %”. Therefore any change to those parameters must be listed under **new** recommendations, not under “already_implemented”.

**Recommendations JSON**

```json

    {
```

**Next immediate action**

- Apply the above parameter changes in the system configuration (environment variables or config file) so that the next ranking (`blofin_rank_opportunities`) uses the new TP/SL, volatility, leverage, and momentum filters.  
- After the changes are live, run a fresh ranking and select the top‑ranked, unblocked symbol (e.g., PTB‑USDT if it meets the new filters) and place a market entry with the new TP/SL defaults (now 6 % / 0.9 %).  
- Log the trade in the journal; the subsequent verification loop will ensure the order ID exists and TP/SL are attached.

**Reflection**

The loop identified that the core obstacle to asymmetric pay‑offs is the overly tight TP and too‑wide SL defaults, plus a lack of volatility filtering. Adjusting these five parameters directly addresses the profit doctrine while respecting existing block/repeat‑loser safeguards. Implementing them now will enable the next cycle to place trades that can capture 5‑10 % moves with ≤1 % downside, delivering the required R ≥ 5:1 profile.

*Ready for the system to apply the recommendations and proceed to the next execution cycle.*

| **Actionable recommendations** | 1. **Refresh symbol universe** – filter out symbols with ≥3 losses or high block counts; focus on those with any positive total PnL or at least a decent avg win (currently none, so wait for a new winner to emerge). <br>2. **Tighten pre‑trade checks** to avoid blocked orders (e.g., verify no open position before placing). <br>3. **Maintain aggressive TP** (5‑10 %+) and tight SL (≈1 %) to force the “big winner pays for small losers” regime. <br>4. **Monitor for any emerging winner** – as soon as a symbol records a win, prioritize it for larger position sizing. |
| **Overall health** | The account is in a **loss‑only** state with many blocked symbols. The strategy is being followed (tight SL, aggressive TP), but **no profitable trades have materialized yet**. Immediate focus should be on expanding the tradable set and catching the first high‑avg‑win symbol. |

---  

**Bottom line:**  
- The system’s guidance is intact, but the current symbol pool yields only losses.  
- Remove repeatedly losing / blocked symbols, tighten order‑placement checks, and wait for a symbol that can deliver a sizable win to kick‑start the asymmetric payoff model.  

---  

*End of Loop 1*
